 Actually, it is not so easy as we see
 agsit pole yaa survey main sample lene kii prakriya kaaphi bojhil hoti he
 Before understanding sampling, we should know exit poll, post poll survey and opinion poll
 kya hote hai agsit pole?agsit pole ke nattejey hameshaa matdaan ke aakhri din hi jari kiye jate hai
 However, data collection is also done on the day of voting
 aakhri phase ke voting ke din jab matadaata vot daalkar nikal rahaa hota he tab usase poocha jaataa he ki usne kise vot diya
 Extensive results are derived from the survey conducted on this basis
 ise hi agsit pole kehete hai
 TV channels usually show exit polls on the last day of voting
 kya hote hai post pole?post pole agsit ke parinaam zyada sateek hote hai
 In the exit poll, soon after the polling, the survey agency gets a rough account of the opinion of the voter
 jabaki post pole hameshaa matdaan ke agle din yaa phir ek-do din baad hote hai
 For example, suppose the 6th phase of voting took place on 12 May
 to survey karne vaali agency matadaataaon se 13, 14, yaa 15 may tak is charan main vot dene vaale matadaataaon se unki raay jaanane kii koshish karen, to ise post pole kaha jaataa he
 Why are post polls more accurate? In exit polls, voters try to get their opinion immediately after voting
 survey karne vaale log poling booth ke baahar hi aisa survey karne karte hai
 Therefore, voters hide their identity in haste and give their opinion, which is not necessarily true
 jabaki post pole main ek din baad voter se baatcheet karke uske man ko tatolane kii koshish kii jaati he ki aakhir usne kis pratyaashee ko mat diya he
 During this time, he is not in any confusion and gives almost correct opinion
 opinian polaopinian pole agsit pole se alag hote hai
 The opinion poll is mostly used by journalists, election survey agencies
 iske jariye patrkaar vibhinn masalon, muddon or chunaavon main janata kii nabj tatolane ke liye kiya karte the
 Credit George Gallup and Claude Robinson were the first to use it
 jaaniye kaise hoti he pole ke liye sampling?opion pole taiyaar karne main sabase bada kaam field work kaa hota he
 For its sampling, the survey agency staff meet the common people and ask some questions
 candidet acha he yaa bura
 On this basis too, a rough opinion is known
 vahiin is prakriya main jin logon ko shaamil kiya jaataa he unhen ek form bhi bharne ko diya jaataa he
 There is also a long process to fill the form
 matadaataaon kii pahchaan gupt rahe or wo bejhijak aapni raay de den
 In such a case, a sealed box is kept for them
 taaki ve apane pasand ke ummidavaar ke bare main bharaa parchaa usamen daal den
 The most important thing in the opinion poll is sampling
 sampling kaa matlab he ki kin logon se raay jaanane kii koshish kii gai he yaa kii jaaegi
 Lok Sabha Elections 2019: Know what the exit polls are, how the statistics are generated, how is the sampling, what is the process? In the opinion poll, only the opinions of some people cannot be concluded
 alag-alag rajyon, vidhaan-sabhaaon or kshetra vishesh kii sampling ke liye methdology alag-alag hogi
 For example, in Madhya Pradesh, Uttar Pradesh and Bihar, the basis of sampling will be different
 kyonki upi or bihar main jis vyakti se uski raay jaanane kii koshish kii jaaegi us vyakti ke saamaajik prishthbhumi, jati or dharm kaa bhi dhyaan rakhana hoga
 If the survey is done keeping in mind the social background, cast and religion, then the sample size of 5000 can also reach the exact conclusion
 jabaki madhyapradesh main jatigat voters kii sampling isse itar hogi
 At the same time, a random sample will be taken according to the percentage of their population in areas with majority Muslim and Dalit population in up-bihar
 kya hoti he random sampling?desh kii badi survey agenciyaan random sampling kaa sahaara leti hai
 It consists of random sampling at the seat, booth level and voter level
 maan lijie kisi booth par 2000 voters hai
 Out of that 100 people have to be interviewed
 to ye 100 log random tareeke se shaamil kiye jaaenge
 For this, two thousand divided by 100, 20 left
 iske baad voter list main se koi ek aisa number random aadhaar par lenge jo 20 se kam ho
 Suppose you took 12
 to voter list main 12wein number par jo matadaata hoga wo pehla sampling candidet hoga jiskaa intervyuu survey agency karegi
 Then 20, 20, 20 are added to that number 12 and the voter is interviewed
 ye hoti random sampling
 What are the means of sampling? To know the opinion poll, a form was also given in the newspapers as well as in the field
 jise bharkar log pate par bhej dete the
 As time changed, technology changed and the method of sampling also changed slightly
 kai survey agenciyaan ab phone colls, esemes online bhi sampling karne lagi hai
 However, phone call sampling is not very effective in the context of India because it is not necessary to get correct information through it
 isiilie intervyuu ke aadhaar par kii gai sampling kamobesh sateek parinaam detii he

 The built Mirage is similar to the 2000, considered by Hindustan Aeronautics Limited as the benchmark for the event
 vimaan kaa pareekshan karne vaala prayek payalat tejas ke flite control system se santusht he, chaahe kalabaji main isaki kushalta ho yaa phir iske flite control system kii risponsiveness
 No pilot has ever suffered any loss in any type of accident during test flights of Tejas
 ab tak isaki 3000 se zyada udaanen safaltaapurvak puri kii ja chuki hai
 Despite these facts, critics say that Tejas is not entirely indigenous
 unka kahana he ki iskaa ingine american he, radar or hathiyaar pranali israeli hai, isaki ijection seat british he, saath hi iske kai anya kalpurje bhi aaayaatit hai
 Hindustan Aeronautics says that aircraft such as France's Rafal and Sweden's Gripen also have foreign systems because developing components is so expensive and too time consuming in the midst of such a fierce competition
 to kya tejas kaarykram ne bharat ke ejineering or vigyaan ke kshetra main koi yogadan diya he? vastav main diya he
 The fly-by-wire system installed at Tejas, which provides computer controlled inputs to control the aircraft, is completely Indian
 vimaan main laga mishan computer, jo sensor se milane vaale data ko process karata he, vah bhi puri tarah bhartiya he
 The hardware and software of the mission computer is designed with the Open Architecture Framework in mind
 iskaa matlab he ki ise bhavishya main apgrade kiya ja saktaa he
 The structure of the aircraft is also made of carbon fiber made in India, which is much lighter and stronger than metal
 yahaan tak ki vimaan main lage saamaanya system jisamen eendhan prabandhan se lekar stearing tak, sab bharat main hi nirmit hai
 An important sensor wave radar, which reports enemy aircraft or ground-to-air missile approaching Tejas, is made in India
 tippaniyan Modern fighter aircraft, including the Indian Air Force's best aircraft Sukhoi 30, are known for their expensive maintenance
 sukhoi 30 kii flit main 60 fisadi se bhi kam vimaan ek vakt par mishan ke liye uplabdh hote hai, jo ki bhartiya vayusena ke liye chintaa kaa vishay he
 HAL says that Tejas will be available for more than 70 per cent of the time, whenever there is a need to go on missions and efforts are on for 80 per cent
 yah vartmaan main vayusena ke kisi bhi vimaan dwaara hasil kiye jane vaale lakshya se kahin zyada he

 tejas kii pareekshan udaanon ke dauraan kisi bhi prakaar kii durghatana main kisi bhi payalat ko kabhi koi nuksaan nahin uthaanaa padaa he

 in tathyon ke baavjood aalochakon kaa kahana he ki tejas puri tarah swadeshi nahin he

 hindustan aironautics kaa kahana he ki france ke rafaal or sweden ke gripan jaise vimaanon main bhi videshi system lage hai kyonki itani kadi pratispardhaa ke bich kalpurjon kaa vikaas karnaa bahut hi mahangaa or bahut hi zyada samay lene vaala hota he

 tejas main laga flani-bai-vir system jo vimaan ko niyantrit karne ke liye computer niyantrit input detaa he, vah puri tarah bhartiya he
 The mission computer mounted on the aircraft, which processes the data from the sensor, is also completely Indian
 mishan computer kaa hardware or software open architekchar fremawork ko dhyaan main rakhkar dizin kiya gaya he
 This means that it can be upgraded in the future
 vimaan kaa dhaancha bhi bharat main bane carbon fibre, jo ki dhaatu kii tulana main kahin zyada halkaa or majboot hota he, se bana he
 Even the common aircraft systems, from fuel management to steering are all manufactured in India
 ek mahatvapurn sensor tarang radar, jo ki dushman ke vimaan yaa jameen se hawa main daagi gai missile ke tejas ke paas aane kii soochna detaa he, bharat main hi bana he
 The comments aadhunik ladaaku vimaan, jisamen bhartiya vayusena kaa sarvshereshth vimaan sukhoi 30 bhi shaamil he, apane mahange rakrakhaav ke liye kukhyat hai
 Less than 60 per cent of aircraft in the Sukhoi 30 fleet are available for missions at one time, which is a concern for the Indian Air Force
 echeel kaa kahana he ki tejas 70 fisadi se zyada samay ke liye uplabdh hoga, jab bhi mishan par jane kii jarurat hogi or 80 fisadi ke liye bhi prayaas jari hai

 farrotedaar english ke liye jaruri tips:1
 Use the search engine in English: When searching any information, use Google in English
 khaskar jab baat ho apni pasand kii khabaren yaa jaankaree hasil karne kii
 For example, if you like cooking, then you should search food recipe in English
 iske alaava fishan, car, travel ke bare main english main jaankaree hasil karen
 At first you may not understand anything, but do not panic
 kuch shabdon ke matlab jaane or phir samajhane kii koshish karen
 Gradually your interest will start increasing
 yahaan free main seekhen english2
 Try to understand by listening: English is considered the best way to learn by listening
 isse sabase bada phayda uccharan sudhaarney main hota he
 So whenever you go out, download some audio recordings of your choice and listen while listening to your headphones
 isse aap english main istemaal hone vaale muhaavarey jaisi kai chizon ke bare main achche se samaj jaaenge
 3
 twitor, fasebuk or google plus par english main post karne vaale logon ko karen follow:fasebuk, twitor or google plus par aap sabhi active honge

 aap us tarah ko logon ko follow karen jo english main post karte hai
 Keep in mind that these people should be from the fields in which you are interested

 After this, you should also communicate with them
 4
 Write your blog in English: You should understand and understand English
 iske liye apni pasand ke hisaab se apana blog banaaen or usamen likhen
 This is a great platform to learn English, with the help of which you can feel free to share your ideas in English
 5
 Also read the blogs of others: If you feel that you are not ready to write your blog at the moment, then you start reading the blogs of others
 blog main aap dekhen ki lekhak kis tarah likh rahaa he, kiske bare main likh rahaa he or log iske blog ko lekar kya-kya coment kar rahe hai
 This will also inspire you and strengthen your writing skills and you will understand the structure of the grammar
 6
 Watch English movies and listen to English music: Who does not like watching movies and listening to songs
 agar aapako english main parfect hona he to aap ye sabhi kaam english main karen
 This will help you learn English
 khaskar aapako aam bolchaal kii bhashaa samajhane main madad milegi
 7
 angreji kitaab padhein:agar aapako kitaaben padhane kaa shauk he to aap apni pasand kii angreji kii kitaab padhein
 For this, keep in mind that read a book that you can read diligently
 shuruyaat main agar ho sake to bacchon kii english kii kitaab padhein
 After this, slowly read your level and English books of choice
 aap angreji bhashaa kaa jo bhi nayaa shabd sikhte hai use ek notebook main likh len
 Also, try to use new words in sentences
 8
 To read the news, follow the English website: It is also very important to know the daily news
 iske liye jaruri he ki aap samachar jaanane ke liye english kii website folon karen
 With this, you will get to read all kinds of news like lifestyle, technology and you will get increased understanding of words in these fields
 9
 Practice with friends: After learning so much in English, you practice speaking with your friends and know how much improvement you have made in English
 10
 Do not translate the language into English: Do not translate your language into English
 fluency ke liye angreji main sochen
 Talk to yourself galtiyaan karne se dare nahin

 pichley maheene pienbi ne bhi maalya ko jaanboojhkar chook karne vaale ghoshit kiya he
 Diageo has to immediately pay $ 40 million to Mallya
 shesh raashi kaa bhugtan samaan kishton main agle paanch saal main kiya janaa he
 In addition, under the deal, Mallya is also exempted from all liabilities related to the alleged financial shortfalls in the company
